< text>
Very nice and relaxing place to start our wine tasting in Calistoga. T-Vine is a collection and preservation of old wineries from historic families who own vineyards. The setup for the wine tasting is great just beside some vineyards and the staff is nice and relaxing. Mostly known for their red wines, enjoy the experience.< /text>

< Review>
We found T-Vine 5 years ago via recommendation after visiting Frank Family and we asked the taster what their favorite winery was.  We were not disappointed. The wines were deeply flavorful and the staff was extremely accommodating even with our 2 small children.  Since then we've been ordering cases from time to time and have never been disappointed.  Occasionally they open up their library wines and I'm able to pick up some birth year wines for my kids.  Looking forward to sharing these wines with them and the stories of visiting Nappa when they were just ankle-biters!  I highly recommend these wines and can't wait to visit when normal times return!< /Review>

My fianc√© and just completed our first weekend stay over in Calistoga and we loved it! We usually stay in or around the Napa area as we have family there, but we decided to give Calistoga a try. On Friday, after a grueling 7-mile hike, we biked from our hotel to T-Vine, our first tasting of the weekend. Boy, what a start! Brendan was our server and not only did he provide amazingly knowledgeable information about the wine, but he also provided a great deal of local information of places for us to check out. Now to the wine! I am a fan of big, juicy reds and there is no shortage of them here. We ended up walking away with 3 tasty bottles including the Mixed Whites bottle, which was a pleasing surprise. Each of the wines opened up in the few moments they sat in the glass and all went down with smooth complexity. We'll highly recommend this to anyone visiting the Calistoga area and particularly if they are lucky enough to have Brendan be your host.</Review>

< Text>
As a former Assistant General Manager at this location some would say that I'm bias but nevertheless this location is the best gym in the bay area. The equipment is in supreme condition, the training staff which roams the floor are more than helpful with any questions one would have regarding technique, advice or proper usage of the equipment. The bathrooms are always clean. They have more than enough space (45000 square feet) to fulfill your workout even at peak hours (Monday -Thursday 5 - 9). The price per month is competitive and relatively a bargain considering most other gyms condition is sub par when thinking about cleanliness. Overall this is a great establishment to further ones health and fitness needs.<//Text>

<review>A very good gym. Wi-Fi now works much better (and Cellular coverage is blocked by the building walls.) Here in Silicon Valley, no Wi-Fi or bad Wi-Fi is unacceptable. There were plenty of Wi-Fi problems until this month, when they got it fixed.

In general, the STAFF is friendly and helpful, but there had been an attitude of "not my job, not my problem" due to upper management not being receptive to ANY sort of constructive criticism about some problems here. It is not the way other CSC locations behave nor should behave. Seems much better now.

Fully equipped with ample free-weights, tons of machines, lots of cardio equipment, ellipticals, treadmills, pool, sauna and spa. Just be sure to bring your own towels (no towel service here) and bring a plastic bag for your wet stuff!

Men‚Äôs lockers can be crowded at peak times. Generally clean but occasionally very messy. Regular staff are generally very friendly and efficient. Cleaning staff has lots of turnover, can be very surly, it seems to me, and cleaning can be atrocious when understaffed and the club is very busy. Trash always overflowing due to door FLAPS on trash cans, not a good design... Toilets and showers may be closed for cleaning during peak times... Then, there are PEAK times when they wet-mop the floor in the locker room. THIS is not good. Wet-mopping should be done off-peak, not during busy times... Then there is also the FREQUENT problem of STANDING DIRTY WATER in many locations in and around the Men's locker room and outside the toilets and passageways -- due to faulty floor construction -- water cannot drain into the floor drains just inches away. STANDING water is unhealthful!

Free passes are available to members online for your friends; limited to several days. I joined a few months ago and got a generous discount for paying in advance. A friendly but often very busy place that offers a lot for regular workouts, especially if you can come in during off-peak times.

< Review>
Pretty awesome gym for the price, which gets you in all City Sports locations in the bay. Same cost as 24-hr but substantially larger/better facilities. Includes squash rooms, pool, basketball court, steam room, you name it. Large locker rooms/showers too that are generally kept pretty clean. The weight selection is good - every machine and barbell setup you can think of in great condition making it easy to do my resistance workouts. Unlike past gyms I've been in, a huge amount of dumbbells (that include 2.5lb increments!) and a huge amount of barbell weights that are kept close to all barbells. I never find myself having to hunt around for weights, to the point where I regularly see staff come around to re-rack or reorganize weights. And there's actually a ton of 2.5lb barbell weights around too - I hated having to hunt for those at other gyms.

The downsides are pretty minor, but enough to knock off a star for me. The smoothie station is often closed/abandoned - apparently they lease this space out to another company, who just show up whenever they feel like it. Pretty disappointing as this was one of the selling points during my trial week (sometimes I'm in a rush and need a quick+cheap bite on the way out). Except for one or two days month, since then I've never seen anyone working there and all the shelves are empty.

Some of the showers in the mens restroom need some TLC - they aren't bad but many soap dispensers don't work at all and/or are frequently watered down.

The "music" they play can be grating at times. This is true for any gym... but what makes it worse here are they play pre-canned jokes for some reason that repeat several times through your workout. It's obnoxious, and can make working out with a partner annoying.

Other than that, awesome gym. It's slightly more expensive than my last rock-bottom price gym but the location is awesome and I get a LOT more out of it.</Review>

<name>Mark Williams</name><Date>1579307246501</Date><rate>1</rate><Review>I'd like to give this place a great review. They run late most of the time like all bus services, but the buses are relatively clean and rarely overly crowded.

But four times now in as many weeks I've witnessed drivers missing stops, three times personally impacting me and another time failing to pick up someone waiting.

When you rely on public transportation on a bus that only runs every 30 minutes it throws your entire trip to or from work when your forced to deal with a 30 minute delay in your trip - every single additional bus or train route has to be adjusted.

It is embarrassing, and shameful to the city of Santa Monica and the obviously unqualified bus drivers that they cannot even drive a simple route once a day without royally screwing up this job. Clearly your driver's are overpaid for the quality of work they are consistently unable to deliver.

We found this place this past weekend.  The crab was excellent, the sauces were interesting and the waitress was great. The only thing not perfect were the utensils  for cracking the crab.  We were only given 1 cracker for breaking the crab shells between us and the splitter was plastic and not very useful at all.  Who likes waiting their turn to use the crab shell pliers  ? Who wants to let their crab get cold? lol not me!!! I think they should supply each person with  their own and upgrade their plastic splitter or give you a pair of scissors as some crab places do.  Other wise the place was great !<//Text>
